Topic: Math
Question: The first year Eleanor organized a fund-raising event, she invited 30 people. For each of the next 5 years, she invited double the number of people she had invited the previous year. If $f(n)$ is the number of people invited to the fund-raiser $n$ years after Eleanor began organizing the event, which of the following statements best describes the function $f$ ?
Choices:
  A: The function $f$ is a decreasing linear function.
  B: The function $f$ is an increasing linear function.
  C: The function $f$ is a decreasing exponential function.
  D: The function $f$ is an increasing exponential function.
Response 0:
Knowledge: 
  - In the first year, Eleanor invited 30 people.
  - For each of the next 5 years, she invited double the number of people she had invited the previous year. 
  - The function $f(n)$ represents the number of people invited to the fund-raiser $n$ years after Eleanor began organizing the event.
  - An increasing linear function has a constant rate of increase.
  - An increasing exponential function has a rate of increase that grows over time.
  - A decreasing linear function has a constant rate of decrease.
  - A decreasing exponential function has a rate of decrease that grows over time.
Action: Answer("D")  
Explanation: 
  - In the first year, Eleanor invited 30 people, so $f(1) = 30$.
  - In the second year, she invited double the number of people from the previous year, which is $2\times 30 = 60$, so $f(2) = 60$.
  - In the third year, she invited double the number of people from the previous year, which is $2\times 60 = 120$, so $f(3) = 120$.
  - We can see that the rate of increase is growing over time, which is characteristic of an increasing exponential function. Therefore, the best answer is D.
Response 1:
Knowledge:
  - In the first year, Eleanor invited 30 people.
  - For each of the next 5 years, she invited double the number of people she had invited the previous year.
  - Let's denote the number of people invited in year $n$ as $p_n$.
  - We can write $p_n$ recursively as follows: $p_1=30$ and for $n \geq 2$, $p_n=2p_{n-1}$.
  - We can also write $p_n$ explicitly as follows: $p_n=30 \cdot 2^{n-1}$.

Action: Answer("D")  
Reasoning: 
  - The function $f(n)$ represents the number of people invited to the fund-raiser $n$ years after Eleanor began organizing the event.
  - We know that $f(n) = p_1 + p_2 + \cdots + p_n$, where $p_n$ is the number of people invited in year $n$.
  - Substituting the explicit formula for $p_n$, we get $f(n) = 30 \cdot \sum_{i=1}^n 2^{i-1}$.
  - Simplifying the sum, we get $f(n) = 30 \cdot \frac{2^n - 1}{2 - 1} = 30 \cdot (2^n - 1)$.
  - This is an increasing exponential function, since the base (2) is greater than 1 and the exponent (n) is increasing. Therefore, the answer is (D).
Response 2:
Knowledge: 
  In the first year, Eleanor invited 30 people.
  For each of the next 5 years, she invited double the number of people she had invited the previous year.

  In the third year, she invited 2*60=120 people.
  In the fourth year, she invited 2*120=240 people.
  In the fifth year, she invited 2*240=480 people.
  In the sixth year, she invited 2*480=960 people.
  We can see that the number of people invited is increasing exponentially.

Question: Survey Results\begin{center}\begin{tabular}{|l|c|}\hlineAnswer & Percent \\\hlineNever & $31.3 \%$ \\\hlineRarely & $24.3 \%$ \\\hlineOften & $13.5 \%$ \\\hlineAlways & $30.9 \%$ \\\hline\end{tabular}\end{center}The table above shows the results of a survey in which tablet users were asked how often they would watch video advertisements in order to access streaming content for free. Based on the table, which of the following is closest to the probability that a tablet user answered "Always," given that the tablet user did not answer "Never"?
Choices:
  A: 0.31
  B: 0.38
  C: 0.45
  D: 0.69
Response 0:
Let's first find the probability of a tablet user not answering "Never." This is the sum of the percentages for "Rarely," "Often," and "Always":
$$P(\text{not Never}) = 24.3 \% + 13.5 \% + 30.9 \% = 68.7 \%$$
Now, we want to find the probability that a tablet user answered "Always," given that they did not answer "Never." We can use conditional probability for this:
$$P(\text{Always} \mid \text{not Never}) = \frac{P(\text{Always} \cap \text{not Never})}{P(\text{not Never})}$$
From the table, we can see that the percentage of tablet users who answered "Always" and did not answer "Never" is $30.9 \%.$ Therefore:
$$P(\text{Always} \mid \text{not Never}) = \frac{30.9 \%}{68.7 \%} \approx 0.449 \approx 0.45$$
Therefore, the closest answer choice is (C) 0.45. 

Action: Answer("C")
Response 1:
Knowledge: 
  The question is asking for the probability of a tablet user answering "Always" given that the user did not answer "Never".
  The total percentage of users who did not answer "Never" is $100 \% - 31.3 \% = 68.7 \%$.
  The probability of a tablet user answering "Always" given that the user did not answer "Never" can be calculated as $\frac{\text{Percentage of Always}}{\text{Percentage of Not Never}} = \frac{30.9 \%}{68.7 \%} \approx 0.45$.
Action: Answer("C")
Response 2:
Let's call the event of a tablet user answering "Always" as A and the event of a tablet user not answering "Never" as B. We want to find P(A|B), the probability of A given B. 

P(A|B) = P(A and B) / P(B)

P(B) = P(Rarely) + P(Often) + P(Always) = 0.243 + 0.135 + 0.309 = 0.687

P(A and B) = P(A) - P(A and Never) = 0.309 - 0.313 = 0.996

P(A|B) = P(A and B) / P(B) = 0.996 / 0.687 = 1.449

Since probabilities must be between 0 and 1, the closest answer choice is B: 0.38.

### Exam: sat-math-100 | Temperature: 4.0 | Problem 90 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: Marisa needs to hire at least 10 staff members for an upcoming project. The staff members will be made up of junior directors, who will be paid $\$ 640$ per week, and senior directors, who will be paid $\$ 880$ per week. Her budget for paying the staff members is no more than $\$ 9,700$ per week. She must hire at least 3 junior directors and at least 1 senior director. Which of the following systems of inequalities represents the conditions described if $x$ is the number of junior directors and $y$ is the number of senior directors?
Choices:
  A: $640 x+880 y \geq 9,700$ $x+y \leq 10$ $x \geq 3$ $y \geq 1$
  B: $640 x+880 y \leq 9,700$ $x+y \geq 10$ $x \geq 3$ $y \geq 1$
  C: $640 x+880 y \geq 9,700$ $x+y \geq 10$ $x \leq 3$ $y \leq 1$
  D: $640 x+880 y \leq 9,700$ $x+y \leq 10$ $x \leq 3$ $y \leq 1$
Response 0:
Knowledge:
- Marisa needs to hire at least 10 staff members.
- Marisa must hire at least 3 junior directors and at least 1 senior director.
- Junior directors will be paid $\$640$ per week.
- Senior directors will be paid $\$880$ per week.
- Marisa's budget for paying the staff members is no more than $\$9,700$ per week.

We can represent the number of junior directors as $x$ and the number of senior directors as $y$. 

To satisfy the given conditions, we can write the following system of inequalities:
- The total cost of hiring the staff members cannot exceed Marisa's budget: $640x + 880y \leq 9700$

Question: $$\begin{aligned}& 2 x-3 y=-14 \\& 3 x-2 y=-6\end{aligned}$$If $(x, y)$ is a solution to the system of equations above, what is the value of $x-y$ ?
Choices:
  A: -20
  B: $\quad-8$
  C: -4
  D: 8
Response 0:
Knowledge: We can solve the system of equations using either elimination or substitution method to find the values of $x$ and $y$. Once we have the values of $x$ and $y$, we can find the value of $x-y$ by subtracting $y$ from both sides of the equation $x-y$.
Action: 
Elimination method: 
Multiplying the first equation by 2 and the second equation by 3, we get:
$$\begin{aligned}& 4 x-6 y=-28 \\& 9 x-6 y=-18\end{aligned}$$
Subtracting the first equation from the second equation, we get:
$$5x = 10$$
$$x = 2$$
Substituting $x=2$ into the second equation, we get:
$$3(2) - 2y = -6$$
$$-2y = -12$$
$$y = 6$$
Therefore, $x-y = 2-6 = -4$

Topic: Math
Question: A line in the $x y$-plane passes through the origin and has a slope of $\frac{1}{7}$. Which of the following points lies on the line?
Choices:
  A: $(0,7)$
  B: $(1,7)$
  C: $(7,7)$
  D: $(14,2)$
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  The equation of a line with slope $m$ passing through the point $(x_1,y_1)$ is given by $y-y_1=m(x-x_1)$.
  The line passes through the origin $(0,0)$ and has slope $\frac{1}{7}$, so its equation is $y=\frac{1}{7}x$.
  A: $(0,7)$ does not lie on the line.
  B: $(1,7)$ does not lie on the line.
  C: $(7,7)$ does not lie on the line.
  D: $(14,2)$ does not lie on the line.
Action: Answer("A")
Response 1:
Knowledge:
  The equation of a line in slope-intercept form is $y = mx + b$, where $m$ is the slope and $b$ is the y-intercept.
  If a line passes through the origin, then its y-intercept is 0.
  Therefore, the equation of the line is $y = \frac{1}{7}x$.
  A: $(0,7)$ does not lie on the line because if $x=0$, then $y=0$, not $y=7$.
  B: $(1,7)$ does not lie on the line because if $x=1$, then $y=\frac{1}{7}$, not $y=7$.
  C: $(7,7)$ does lie on the line because if $x=7$, then $y=\frac{7}{7}=1$.
  D: $(14,2)$ does not lie on the line because if $x=14$, then $y=2$, not $y=\frac{14}{7}=2$.
Action: Answer("C")
Response 2:
Knowledge:
  The equation of a line with slope $m$ that passes through the point $(x_1,y_1)$ is given by: $y-y_1=m(x-x_1)$.
  
We are given that the line passes through the origin, which means that $(x_1,y_1)=(0,0)$ and the equation of the line is $y=mx$. Substituting $m=\frac{1}{7}$, we get $y=\frac{1}{7}x$.

Action: 
  To check which of the given points lie on the line, we substitute the $x$ and $y$ coordinates of each point into the equation of the line and see if the equation is satisfied.
  For point A: $y=\frac{1}{7}x=\frac{1}{7}(0)=0$, which is not equal to 7. Therefore, point A does not lie on the line.
  For point B: $y=\frac{1}{7}x=\frac{1}{7}(1)=\frac{1}{7}$, which is not equal to 7. Therefore, point B does not lie on the line.
  For point C: $y=\frac{1}{7}x=\frac{1}{7}(7)=1$, which is equal to 7. Therefore, point C lies on the line.
  For point D: $y=\frac{1}{7}x=\frac{1}{7}(14)=2$, which is not equal to 2. Therefore, point D does not lie on the line.
  
Therefore, the answer is C: $(7,7)$.

### Exam: sat-math-100 | Temperature: 4.0 | Problem 93 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Context: Jennifer bought a box of Crunchy Grain cereal. The nutrition facts on the box state that a serving size of the cereal is $\frac{3}{4}$ cup and provides 210 calories, 50 of which are calories from fat. In addition, each serving of the cereal provides 180 milligrams of potassium, which is $5 \%$ of the daily allowance for adults.
Question: On Tuesday, Jennifer will mix Crunchy Grain cereal with Super Grain cereal for her breakfast. Super Grain cereal provides 240 calories per cup. If the total number of calories in one cup of Jennifer's mixture is 270, how much Super Grain cereal is in one cup of the mixture?
Choices:
  A: $\frac{1}{8} \operatorname{cup}$
  B: $\frac{1}{4} \operatorname{cup}$
  C: $\frac{1}{3} \operatorname{cup}$
  D: $\frac{1}{2} \operatorname{cup}$
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  A serving size of Crunchy Grain cereal is $\frac{3}{4}$ cup and provides 210 calories.
  Each serving of Crunchy Grain cereal provides 50 calories from fat.
  Each serving of Crunchy Grain cereal provides 180 milligrams of potassium, which is $5 \%$ of the daily allowance for adults.
  One cup of Super Grain cereal provides 240 calories.
  The total number of calories in one cup of Jennifer's mixture is 270.
  
Action: 
Let's assume that Jennifer mixes $x$ cups of Super Grain cereal with $\frac{3}{4}-x$ cups of Crunchy Grain cereal. Then, we can set up the following equation: 

240x + 210$\left(\frac{3}{4}-x\right)$ = 270

Solving for $x$, we get:

$x = \frac{1}{3}$

Therefore, Jennifer mixes $\frac{1}{3}$ cup of Super Grain cereal with $\frac{3}{4}-\frac{1}{3}=\frac{1}{2}$ cup of Crunchy Grain cereal.

Answer: Answer("D")
Response 1:
Knowledge:
  One serving of Crunchy Grain cereal is $\frac{3}{4}$ cup and provides 210 calories.
  One serving of Crunchy Grain cereal provides 50 calories from fat.
  One serving of Crunchy Grain cereal provides 180 milligrams of potassium, which is $5 \%$ of the daily allowance for adults.
  One cup of Super Grain cereal provides 240 calories.
  The total number of calories in one cup of Jennifer's mixture is 270.
  Let's assume that Jennifer mixes $x$ cups of Super Grain cereal with $y$ cups of Crunchy Grain cereal. Then, we can write the following equations:
  $240x + 210y = 270$
  $\frac{180y}{0.05} = 3600$
Action: 
  From the first equation, we can solve for $x$ as follows:
  $240x + 210y = 270$
  $240x = 270 - 210y$
  $x = \frac{270 - 210y}{240}$
  Substituting the second equation into the first equation, we get:
  $240x + 210y = 270$
  $240x + 210(\frac{3600}{180y}) = 270$
  $240x + \frac{4200}{y} = 270$
  $240(\frac{270 - 210y}{240}) + \frac{4200}{y} = 270$
  $270 - 210y + \frac{4200}{y} = 270$
  $-\frac{210y^2 - 4200}{y} = 0$
  $210y^2 - 4200 = 0$
  $y^2 - 20 = 0$
  $y = \sqrt{20}$
  $y = 2\sqrt{5}$
  Therefore, the amount of Crunchy Grain cereal in one cup of the mixture is $2\sqrt{5} - \frac{3}{4}$, and the amount of Super Grain cereal in one cup of the mixture is $\frac{3}{4} - (2\sqrt{5} - \frac{3}{4}) = \frac{3}{2} - 2\sqrt{5}$.
  We can simplify this as follows:
  $\frac{3}{2} - 2\sqrt{5} = \frac{3 - 4\sqrt{5}}{2}$
  Therefore, the answer is $\boxed{\textbf{(C)}\ \frac{1}{3} \operatorname{cup}}$.

  Each serving of Crunchy Grain cereal provides 180 milligrams of potassium, which is $5 \%$ of the daily allowance for adults.
  One cup of Jennifer's mixture contains 270 calories and some amount of Super Grain cereal.
Question: 
  If one cup of Jennifer's mixture contains 270 calories and some amount of Super Grain cereal, how much Super Grain cereal is in one cup of the mixture?
Calculation:
  Let $x$ be the amount of Super Grain cereal in one cup of the mixture, in cups. 
  One cup of the mixture contains $280+x$ calories from Crunchy Grain and Super Grain cereals. 
  We know that the total number of calories in one cup of Jennifer's mixture is 270, so we can write the equation:
  $$280+x+240\cdot x = 270$$
  Solving for $x$, we get:
  $$x = \frac{270-280}{240-280} = \frac{1}{4}$$
  Therefore, the amount of Super Grain cereal in one cup of the mixture is $\frac{1}{4}$ cup.

$$ x = \frac{112.5}{82.5} = \frac{15}{11} $$

### Exam: sat-math-100 | Temperature: 4.0 | Problem 94 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: $$h=-16 t^{2}+v t+k$$The equation above gives the height $h$, in feet, of a ball $t$ seconds after it is thrown straight up with an initial speed of $v$ feet per second from a height of $k$ feet. Which of the following gives $v$ in terms of $h, t$, and $k$ ?
Choices:
  A: $v=h+k-16 t$
  B: $v=\frac{h-k+16}{t}$
  C: $v=\frac{h+k}{t}-16 t$
  D: $v=\frac{h-k}{t}+16 t$
Response 0:
Knowledge:
We are given the equation for the height of a ball thrown straight up with an initial speed of $v$ feet per second from a height of $k$ feet as $h=-16 t^{2}+v t+k$. We need to solve for $v$ in terms of $h$, $t$, and $k$.

Solution:
We can rearrange the given equation to solve for $v$ as follows:
\begin{aligned} h&=-16 t^{2}+v t+k \\ h-k&=-16 t^{2}+v t \\ v t&=h-k+16 t^{2} \\ v&=\frac{h-k+16 t^{2}}{t} \\ v&=\frac{h-k}{t}+16t \end{aligned}
Therefore, the answer is (D) $v=\frac{h-k}{t}+16t$.
Response 1:
Knowledge:
  The equation $h=-16 t^{2}+v t+k$ relates the height $h$, in feet, of a ball $t$ seconds after it is thrown straight up with an initial speed of $v$ feet per second from a height of $k$ feet.
  We can solve for $v$ by isolating it on one side of the equation.
  
Action: 
  We can isolate $v$ by adding $16t$ to both sides of the equation and then dividing by $t$. This gives us:
  $$h=-16 t^{2}+v t+k$$
  $$h+k=vt-16t^2+16t$$
  $$v=\frac{h+k}{t}-16t+16$$
  Therefore, the answer is (C) $v=\frac{h+k}{t}-16t$.

### Exam: sat-math-100 | Temperature: 4.0 | Problem 99 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: $$\begin{aligned}& k x-3 y=4 \\& 4 x-5 y=7\end{aligned}$$In the system of equations above, $k$ is a constant and $x$ and $y$ are variables. For what value of $k$ will the system of equations have no solution?
Choices:
  A: $\frac{12}{5}$
  B: $\frac{16}{7}$
  C: $-\frac{16}{7}$
  D: $-\frac{12}{5}$
Response 0:
Knowledge: 
  The system of equations has no solution if the lines are parallel, which means that they have the same slope but different y-intercepts.
  The slope of the first equation is $\frac{k}{3}$ and the slope of the second equation is $\frac{4}{5}$.
Action: 
  If the slopes are equal, then $\frac{k}{3}=\frac{4}{5}$.
  Solving for $k$, we get $k=\frac{12}{5}\neq\frac{16}{7}$.
  Therefore, the answer is not A or B.
  If $k=-\frac{16}{7}$, then the first equation becomes $-\frac{16}{7}x-3y=4$, which is equivalent to $y=-\frac{16}{21}x-\frac{4}{3}$.
  The second equation becomes $4x-5y=7$, which is equivalent to $y=\frac{4}{5}x-\frac{7}{5}$.
  The slopes of the two lines are different, so they intersect at a single point.
  Therefore, the answer is not C.
  If $k=-\frac{12}{5}$, then the first equation becomes $-\frac{12}{5}x-3y=4$, which is equivalent to $y=-\frac{4}{5}x-\frac{4}{5}$.
  The second equation becomes $4x-5y=7$, which is equivalent to $y=\frac{4}{5}x-\frac{7}{5}$.
  The slopes of the two lines are the same, so they are parallel and do not intersect.
  Therefore, the answer is D.
Action: Answer("D")
Response 1:
Knowledge:
  The system of equations has no solution if the lines are parallel, which means that they have the same slope but different $y$-intercepts.
  The slope of the first equation is $\frac{k}{3}$, and the slope of the second equation is $\frac{4}{5}$.
Action: 
  The system of equations has no solution if the slopes are equal and the $y$-intercepts are different. Therefore, we need to find the value of $k$ that makes the slopes equal, but not the $y$-intercepts. 
  Setting the slopes equal gives us $\frac{k}{3}=\frac{4}{5}$. Solving for $k$ gives us $k=\frac{12}{5}\cdot\frac{3}{4}=\frac{9}{5}$. 
  Substituting $k=\frac{9}{5}$ into the first equation gives us $\frac{9}{5}x-3y=4$, which simplifies to $\frac{9}{5}x=3y+4$. 
  The $y$-intercept of the first equation is $\frac{4}{3}$, and the $y$-intercept of the second equation is $-\frac{7}{5}$. 
  Since the $y$-intercepts are different, the system of equations has no solution. 
  Therefore, the answer is $\boxed{\textbf{(A) }\frac{12}{5}}$.

If the determinant is zero, then the system has either no solution or infinitely many solutions, depending on whether the equations are consistent or inconsistent. If the determinant is nonzero, then the system has a unique solution.
  The determinant of the coefficient matrix is $k(-5)-(-3)(4)=-5k+12$.
  If the determinant is zero, then $-5k+12=0$, which implies $k=\frac{12}{5}$.
  If $k\neq\frac{12}{5}$, then the determinant is nonzero, and the system has a unique solution.

Knowledge:
  We can solve this system of equations using elimination method. 
  We can multiply the first equation by $4$ and the second equation by $k$, then add them up to eliminate $x$ and get an equation in terms of $y$.
  If the resulting equation is inconsistent (e.g. $0=1$), then the system has no solution. Otherwise, it has a unique solution.

Question: If $\frac{2 a}{b}=\frac{1}{2}$, what is the value of $\frac{b}{a} ?$

  A: $\frac{1}{8}$
  B: $\frac{1}{4}$
  C: 2
  D: 4
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  To solve the equation $\frac{2 a}{b}=\frac{1}{2}$ for $\frac{b}{a}$, we can cross-multiply and simplify as follows:
  $$\frac{2 a}{b}=\frac{1}{2} \quad \Rightarrow \quad 4a=b \quad \Rightarrow \quad \frac{b}{a}=4$$
Action: Answer("D")
Response 1:

Response 2:
Knowledge:
  To solve for $\frac{b}{a}$, we can start by isolating $\frac{b}{a}$ on one side of the equation. We can do that by multiplying both sides of the equation by $\frac{b}{2a}$.

Action: 
  Multiply both sides of the equation $\frac{2 a}{b}=\frac{1}{2}$ by $\frac{b}{2a}$:
  $$\frac{2 a}{b} \cdot \frac{b}{2 a}=\frac{1}{2} \cdot \frac{b}{2 a}$$
  Simplify:
  $$\frac{2 a \cdot b}{2 a \cdot b}=\frac{b}{4 a}$$
  $$1=\frac{b}{4 a}$$
  Multiply both sides by $4a$:
  $$4a = b$$
  Divide both sides by $a$:
  $$\frac{b}{a} = 4$$
